1454
1455 struct KeyType {
1456 uint16_t Encoding;
1457 };
1458 KeyType Key = {Encoding};
1459 auto Table = makeArrayRef(Index);
1460 auto Idx = std::lower_bound(Table.begin(), Table.end(), Key,
1461 [](const IndexType &LHS, const KeyType &RHS) {
1462 if (LHS.Encoding < RHS.Encoding)
1463 return true;
1464 if (LHS.Encoding > RHS.Encoding)
1465 return false;
1466 return false;
1467 });
1468
1469 if (Idx == Table.end() ||
1470 Key.Encoding != Idx->Encoding)
1471 return nullptr;
1472 return &TLBITable[Idx->_index];
1473}

4815 { "ZCR_EL3", 743 },
4816 };
4817
4818 struct KeyType {
4819 std::string Name;
4820 };
4821 KeyType Key = {Name.upper()};
4822 auto Table = makeArrayRef(Index);
4823 auto Idx = std::lower_bound(Table.begin(), Table.end(), Key,
4824 [](const IndexType &LHS, const KeyType &RHS) {
4825 int CmpName = StringRef(LHS.Name).compare(RHS.Name);
4826 if (CmpName < 0) return true;
4827 if (CmpName > 0) return false;
4828 return false;
4829 });
4830
4831 if (Idx == Table.end() ||
4832 Key.Name != Idx->Name)
4833 return nullptr;
4834 return &SysRegsList[Idx->_index];
4835}

5762
5763 struct KeyType {
5764 uint16_t Encoding;
5765 };
5766 KeyType Key = {Encoding};
5767 auto Table = makeArrayRef(Index);
5768 auto Idx = std::lower_bound(Table.begin(), Table.end(), Key,
5769 [](const IndexType &LHS, const KeyType &RHS) {
5770 if (LHS.Encoding < RHS.Encoding)
5771 return true;
5772 if (LHS.Encoding > RHS.Encoding)
5773 return false;
5774 return false;
5775 });
5776
5777 if (Idx == Table.end() ||
5778 Key.Encoding != Idx->Encoding)
5779 return nullptr;
5780 return &SysRegsList[Idx->_index];
5781}

5785const TSB *lookupTSBByName(StringRef Name);

5789#ifdef GET_TSB_IMPL
5790constexpr TSB TSBsList[] = {
5791 { "csync", 0x0, {AArch64::FeatureTRACEV8_4} }, // 0
5792 };
5793
5794const TSB *lookupTSBByName(StringRef Name) {
5795 struct IndexType {
5796 const char * Name;
5797 unsigned _index;
5798 };
5799 static const struct IndexType Index[] = {
5800 { "CSYNC", 0 },
5801 };
5802
5803 struct KeyType {
5804 std::string Name;
5805 };
5806 KeyType Key = {Name.upper()};
5807 auto Table = makeArrayRef(Index);
5808 auto Idx = std::lower_bound(Table.begin(), Table.end(), Key,
5809 [](const IndexType &LHS, const KeyType &RHS) {
5810 int CmpName = StringRef(LHS.Name).compare(RHS.Name);
5811 if (CmpName < 0) return true;
5812 if (CmpName > 0) return false;
5813 return false;
5814 });
5815
5816 if (Idx == Table.end() ||
5817 Key.Name != Idx->Name)
5818 return nullptr;
5819 return &TSBsList[Idx->_index];
5820}
5821
5822const TSB *lookupTSBByEncoding(uint8_t Encoding) {
5823 struct IndexType {
5824 uint8_t Encoding;
5825 unsigned _index;
5826 };
5827 static const struct IndexType Index[] = {
5828 { 0x0, 0 },
5829 };
5830
5831 auto Table = makeArrayRef(Index);
5832 size_t Idx = Encoding;
5833 return Idx >= Table.size() ? nullptr : &TSBsList[Table[Idx]._index];
5834}
